%%Series with alternating signs are a little more challenging. This series sums to
%ln (2) (the natural logarithm of 2): 1-1/2+1/3-1/4+1/5-.......
delete sum_of_first_9999_terms.txt
diary  sum_of_first_9999_terms.txt
echo on
sign = -1;
s=0;
for n = 1:9999
sign = -sign;
s=s+sign / n
end
echo off
diary off

s=0;

sign = -sign;
s=s+sign / n
